Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Candidates applying for the post of Executive Director 
(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Candidates applying for the post of Executive Director 
(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Candidates applying for the post of Executive Director 
(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo

proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of

Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo

employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates appointed on Deputation basis would 
have the option to draw pay and allowances as 
admissible to him/her in the parent organization or the 
scale of pay as admissible in SEBI.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Candidates applying for the post of Executive Director 
(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo

Manager may also apply for position of Executive

eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview.

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

1. Mode of Selection will be Interview. To widen the 
pool of suitable candidates for appointment to the

a search-cum-selection process. The Board reserves 
the right to modify the selection procedure, if

Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

1. Mode of Selection will be Interview. To widen the 
pool of suitable candidates for appointment to the

a search-cum-selection process. The Board reserves 
the right to modify the selection procedure, if

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Manager may also apply for position of Executive

eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The

from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

1. Mode of Selection will be Interview. To widen the 
pool of suitable candidates for appointment to the 
post of Executive Director, the Board will also follow 
a search-cum-selection process. The Board reserves 
the right to modify the selection procedure, if

Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI / 
Board), is a statutory regulatory body established by 
an Act of Parliament, to protect the interests of 
investors in securities, to promote the development of 
and to regulate the securities market. SEBI invites 
applications from Indian citizens for the post of 
Executive Director on contract/ deputation basis. αñòαñ╛αñ░αÑìαñ»αñ¬αñ╛αñ▓αñò αñ¿αñ┐αñªαÑçαñ╢αñò ΓÇô αñ¬αñªαÑïαñé αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñé.: 1 (αñÅαñò)

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo

proper discharge certificate from the previous

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Manager may also apply for position of Executive

eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The

from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ

(On Contract) who are already in service of 
Govt./Quasi-Govt. Organizations and Public Sector 
Banks/Undertakings will have to produce a ΓÇÿNo 
Objection Certificate' from their employer, on or before 
the date of Interview. Before appointment in SEBI, a 
proper discharge certificate from the previous 
employer will also have to be produced. αñ»αñ╣αñª αñ½αñòαñ╕αÑÇ αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ▓αñÅ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñëαñ╕αñòαÑÇ αñ╕αñ╛αñéαñ╕αÑìαñÑαñ╛ (αñëαñ╕αñòαÑç

Note: Officers of SEBI in the rank of Chief General 
Manager may also apply for position of Executive 
Director on contract basis subject to fulfilling above 
eligibility criteria. The candidature of such Officers will 
be considered strictly on suitability and merit. The 
candidate, if selected, shall be required to resign/retire 
from the services of the Board. However, preference 
will be given to external candidate for the advertised 
post. αñ¬αÑìαñ░αñ¿αñ░αÑìαññαñ¿αñ┐αñ░αÑìαÑüαñ╕αÑìαñòαÑìαñ░αÑìαññ αñåαñºαñ╛αñ░ αñ¬αñ░ [αñ╕αñ░αñòαñ╛αñ░, αñ¡αñ╛αñ░αñ░αÑìαññαÑÇαñ░αÑì αñ░αñ░αñ£αñ╝αñ╡αñ» αñ¼αÑêαñéαñò, αñ¼αÑêαñéαñòαÑïαñé,

The candidates applying for the post of Executive 
Director on Deputation basis should route their 
application through the employer. Such candidates 
should submit an 'Advance Copy' of their application 
to SEBI through the online link on or before the last 
date of application as given in the advertisement. The 
application in hard copy should be routed through the 
employer which should reach SEBI on or before the 
date of interview. αñÉαñ╕αÑç αñëαñ«αÑìαñ«αÑÇαñªαñ┐αñ╛αñ░ αñåαñ┐αÑçαñªαñ┐ αñòαÑç αñ╕αñ╛αñÑ αñ╕αññαñòαñíαññαñ╛ αñ╡αñ┐αñ¡αñ╛αñù αñòαÑç αñàαñ┐αñ╛αñ¬αñ£αññαÑìαññ
